country_event = { # Strike
	id = ukrpol.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.6" }
	title = ukrpol.6.t
	desc = ukrpol.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_strike

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
			}
		}
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_minor_concessions
			days = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.07
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike
			days = 14
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_workers_loves_dyrektoria
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 1
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		UKR_increase_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike_big
			days = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_workers_loves_dyrektoria
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			UKR_decrease_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Dualism
	id = ukrpol.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.10" }
	title = ukrpol.10.t
	desc = ukrpol.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_DEM  }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_COSSACK  }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_AUT  }
				}
			}
		}			
		set_country_flag = UKR_king_path
		complete_national_focus = UKR_King_Path
		add_ideas = UKR_dualism
		set_variable = { political_power_ideology = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		map_party_popularity_PP_gain_to_ideology = yes
		set_power_balance = {
			id = UKR_dualism
			left_side = UKR_king_side 
			right_side = UKR_hetman_side
			set_value = 0.05
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.12
			days = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_SOCIALISM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_MONSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE_MONARCH }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN_DEMOCRACY }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_JUNTA }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_OTAMANOVSKYI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UMP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_USKHD }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_KON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_MELNYK }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_DONTSOV }
				}
			}
		}			
		set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
		complete_national_focus = UKR_Hetman_Path
		add_ideas = UKR_dualism
		set_power_balance = {
			id = UKR_dualism
			left_side = UKR_king_side 
			right_side = UKR_hetman_side

country_event = { # Melnyk Returns
	id = ukrpol.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.13" }
	title = ukrpol.13.t
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.13.d.king
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_King_Path }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.13.d.hetman
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = UKR_King_Path }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_melnyk
	
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.13.a
		set_global_flag = WSU_totalist_uvo
		UPR = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 17905 }
				set_nationality = ROOT
				clr_unit_leader_flag = UVO_Galicia_leader
			}
		}
		UPR = {
			clr_country_flag = UPR_melnyk_on_our_side
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 17917 }
					promote_leader = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = will_become_uvo_leader_galicia
					set_unit_leader_flag = UVO_Galicia_leader
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = leftist_uvo_becomes_dominant_galicia
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Stsiborskyi"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_STSIBORSKYI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Stsiborskyi.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = red_tinted_autocracy_subtype

			hidden_effect = {

					name = UKR_totalist_party3
					long_name = UKR_totalist_party3_long

country_event = { # End of the Hetmanate
	id = ukrpol.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.25" }
	title = ukrpol.25.t
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.25.d.uvo
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.25.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_lypky
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = UKR
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		OR = {
			power_balance_value = {
				id = UKR_dualism
				value < 0
			}
			check_variable = { UKR_society_support > 0 }
		}
		NOT = { 
			power_balance_value = {
				id = UKR_dualism
				value > 0
			} 
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.25.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path }
			clr_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
			set_country_flag = UKR_king_path
		}
		default_party_popularity_PP_gain = yes
		UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
		UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		remove_power_balance = { id = UKR_dualism }
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 17909 }
				retire = yes
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		remove_ideas = UKR_derzhavna_varta
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO
					has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_Wih_UDP
				}
			}
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Vasyl_Vyshyvanyi_hog_ade
				UKR_Kazymyr_Huzhkovskyi_for_ade
				UKR_Omelian_Senyk_eco_npo
				UKR_Dmitri_Dontsov_sec_npo
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.34
				days = 3
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				end_coalition = yes
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Vyacheslav_Lypynskyi_hog_ade
				UKR_Serhiy_Shemet_for_ade
				UKR_Mykhailo_Savur_Tsypriianovych_eco_ade
				UKR_Yulian_Romanchuk_sec_ade
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.152
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.150
				days = 20
				random_days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.90
				days = 4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_become_exiled_in_WSU
					NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_dyrektoria_uprising_active }
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = UKR_dualism
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_dualism
					add_idea = UKR_political_instability
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = UKR_UMP_USKhD_Coalition
		set_variable = { UKR_maximum_alignment = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_uskhd_cons = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_uskhd_lib = 0 }
		recalculate_ukrainian_political_variables = yes
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 17909 }
				set_nationality = XXA
			}
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = ukrpol.76
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = Pavlo_Skoropadskyi_dead
	}						
}

	id = ukrpol.150

	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.150.d.upss
		trigger = { UKR_upss_in_power = yes }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.150.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_CHOOSE_HEIR option = UKR_CHOOSE_HEIR_SKOROPADSKY }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_SOCIALISM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_JUNTA }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_OTAMANOVSKYI }
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		set_country_flag = UKR_LEO
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = UKR_GER_stefan_hab
		} # -20
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = UKR_AUS_stefan_hab
		} # 30
		if = {
			limit = { UKR_upss_in_power = yes }
			UKR_triumvirs_increase_bolbochan = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.150.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				UKR_upss_in_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_CHOOSE_HEIR option = UKR_CHOOSE_HEIR_HABSBURG }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_SOCIALISM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_CONSERVATIVE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_JUNTA }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_HREKIV_OTAMANOVSKYI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_FUTURE option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UPSS_BOLBOCHAN_DEMOCRACY }
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
		set_country_flag = UKR_DAN
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = UKR_GER_daniil_sko
		} # 20
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = UKR_AUS_daniil_sko
		} # -30
		if = {
			limit = { UKR_upss_in_power = yes }
			UKR_triumvirs_increase_shapoval = yes

	desc = ukrpol.630.d

		name = ukrpol.630.a
		remove_ideas = UKR_hetman_abdicated

			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_unit_leader = 17913 }
				}
				XXA = {
					random_unit_leader = {
						limit = { has_id = 17913 }
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.12
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.08
			}
		}	
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ivan Poltavets-Ostrianytsia"
			desc = "POLITICS_IVAN_POLTAVETS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Ivan_Poltavets_Ostrianytsia.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = pataut_cossack_subtype
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Kozatska Dyviziia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Kozatska Dyviziia"
				division_names_group = UKR_CAV_02
				regiments = {
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}

				set_party_name = { ideology = national_populist name = UKR_national_populist_party2 }
				set_party_name = { ideology = paternal_autocrat name = UKR_national_populist_party5 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					name = UKR_national_populist_party4
					long_name = UKR_national_populist_party4_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = UKR_national_populist_party5
					long_name = UKR_national_populist_party5_long
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Andriy Melnyk"
					desc = "POLITICS_ANDRIY_MELNYK_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Andriy_Melnyk_Extra.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = junta_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { UKR_sun_integralists = 0 }
			set_variable = { UKR_sun_nrm = 0.35 }
			set_variable = { UKR_sun_old_guard = 0.65 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_party_name = { ideology = national_populist name = UKR_national_populist_party2 }
				set_party_name = { ideology = paternal_autocrat name = UKR_national_populist_party2 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					name = UKR_national_populist_party2
					long_name = UKR_national_populist_party2_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = UKR_national_populist_party2
					long_name = UKR_national_populist_party2_long
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_SUN_syndicalized }
			set_country_leader_ideology = right_syndicalism_subtype
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
			add_ideas = UKR_Kirill_Osmak_eco_tot
		}
		else = {
			set_country_leader_ideology = ukrainian_nationalism_subtype
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_nationalist
		random_other_country = {
			news_event = {
				id = ukrsun.13
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsun.24
				days = 60
				random_days = 60
			}
		}
	}			
}

country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.69
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.69" }
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.t.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.69.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_global_flag = KCN_economic_yes
		KCN_add_to_kcn_economic = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }
			}
			country_event = ukrsoc.71
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					OR = {
						GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
						is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
						is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.70 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
							is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
							is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.71 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.69.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}	
}

	id = ukrsoc.70
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.70" }
	title = ukrsoc.70.t
	desc = ukrsoc.70.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.70.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
					is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
					is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
				}
			}
		}			
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_1
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_2
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_3
			}
		}
		GER_leave_mitteleuropa = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_withdraws_from_sphere
			hidden_effect = { country_event = japfor.404 }
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_outraged }
				country_event = japfor.409
			}
			remove_ideas = JAP_nav_tra_idea
		}
		KCN_add_to_kcn_economic = yes
	}	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.70.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
					is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
					is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
				}
			}
		}		
	}

country_event = { #Membership - voting
	id = ukrsoc.77
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.77 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.77.t
	desc = ukrsoc.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = KCN_vote_yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = KCN_vote_no
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = KCN_vote_abstain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Membership - voting
	id = ukrsoc.85
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.85 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.85.t
	desc = ukrsoc.85.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = KCN_vote_yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = KCN_vote_no
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = KCN_vote_abstain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.87
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.87" }
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.87.t.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.87.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.87.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.87.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }

		event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = {

		}
		clear_global_event_target = KCN_candidate_membership
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.87.c

			check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes }

		}

		}

	}

country_event = { # UKP 
	id = ukrsoc.113
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.113" }
	title = ukrsoc.113.t
	desc = ukrsoc.113.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.113.a
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
			}
			INT = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			give_guarantee = FROM
			FROM = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { has_government = totalist }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = UKR_radical_socialist_party
				long_name = UKR_radical_socialist_party_long
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Skrypnyk"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_SKRYPNYK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Skrypnyk.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_communism_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.117
				days = 180
				random_days = 300
			}
		}
	}		
}

country_event = { # USDRP
	id = ukrsoc.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.152" }
	title = ukrsoc.152.t
	desc = ukrsoc.152.d
	trigger = {
		UKR_usdrp_in_power = yes	
	}
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget > 0 }
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 11 }
			}
			check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = -10 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School
				days = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.152
				days = 90
				random_days = 220
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_Borrow_money_tt
		add_to_variable = { var = UKR_kyiv_budget_debt value = 40 }
		multiply_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget_debt = 1.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Repay_money
				days = 180
			}
		}
		else = { activate_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}		
		set_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = 5 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_monthly_change = -5 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_monthly_by_sum = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			remove_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
		}		
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_change = 40 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_by_sum = yes
	}		
}

		name = ukrsoc.207.a
		army_experience = 30

			limit = { has_idea = Hetman_army }
			remove_ideas = Hetman_army
		}
		complete_national_focus = UKR_Povstanarmia
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Ukrainska Radianska Dyviziia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Ukrainska Radianska Dyviziia"
				division_names_group = USR_INF_01
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Ukrainska Radianska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 3
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Ukrainska Radianska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}

				count = 2
			}
		}
	}

		}

				destroy_unit = yes
			}

			}
		}

		}
	}

			limit = { has_id = 1962 }

		}

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Kozatska Dyviziia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Kozatska Dyviziia"
				division_names_group = UKR_CAV_02
				regiments = {
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 2
			}
		}
	}		
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.250" }

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1233

					state = 1229

					state = 240
					state = 203
					state = 259
					state = 221
					state = 227
					state = 228

					state = 1284
					state = 1285
					state = 1286
					state = 226
					state = 1231
					state = 200
					state = 1239
					state = 197
					state = 196	
				}
			}
			set_border_war = yes
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = UKR_borotbyst_uprising_state
			}
		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.251
				days = 5
			}
		}				
	}	
}

	id = ukrsoc.252
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.252" }
	title = ukrsoc.252.t
	desc = ukrsoc.252.d
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.252.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 15 
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000

					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_PEOPLES_REPUBLIC option = UKR_FUTURE_PETLIURA_SHUMSKYI }

				type = contain
				id = "UPR"
				value = -200
			}

				type = conquer
				id = "UPR"
				value = -500
			}

				type = antagonize
				id = "UPR"
				value = -200
			}
		}

			mission = UKR_war_with_borotbysts

		}
	}

		remove_ideas = UKR_borotbyst_uprising

			base = 40 
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000

			}
		}
		UKR_setup_petliura_melnyk_diarchy = yes

country_event = { # Agricultural crisis!
	id = ukreco.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukreco.2" }
	title = ukreco.2.t
	desc = ukreco.2.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukreco.2.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = UKR_GER_no_help_agr_crisis
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.25
		set_country_flag = UKR_agriculture_crisis

				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Borotbysts < 30 }
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_revolution option = UKR_REVOLUTION_DISABLED }
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Popularity > 75 }
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Success > 75 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_redistribution_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Socialization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_socialization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Municipalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_municipalization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_Nationalization_Land 
						has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land
					}
				}
				add_ideas = UKR_nationalisation_of_land
			}
			else = { 
				add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_excellent
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_resource_penalty = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Popularity > 50 }
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Success > 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_redistribution_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Socialization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_socialization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Municipalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_municipalization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_Nationalization_Land 
						has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land
					}
				}
				add_ideas = UKR_nationalisation_of_land
			}
			else = { 
				add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_good 
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SUN_redistribution_land }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_trade_opinion = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Socialization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_socialization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Municipalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_municipalization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_Nationalization_Land 
						has_country_flag = SUN_nationalization_land
					}
				}
				add_ideas = UKR_nationalisation_of_land
			}
			else = { add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_decent }
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_LandReform_Success
		set_country_flag = UKR_disable_borotbist_uprisings
		clr_country_flag = LandReformBegunUKR
		remove_ideas = UKR_land_reform
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_land_reform_modifier }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = UKR_borotbyst_uprising_state
				}
			}
			set_border_war = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = UKR_borotbyst_uprising_state
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukreco.25.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Borotbysts > 29 }
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_revolution option = UKR_REVOLUTION_GUARANTEED }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_revolution option = UKR_REVOLUTION_CIVIL_WAR }
						has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_revolution option = UKR_REVOLUTION_COUP }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		clr_country_flag = LandReformBegunUKR
		remove_ideas = UKR_land_reform
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_land_reform_modifier }
		country_event = {
			id = ukrsoc.200
			days = 5
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = { # WHR & UKR are independent
	id = ukrfor.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.11" }
	title = ukrfor.11.t
	desc = ukrfor.11.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = UKR
		UKR = {
			is_subject = no
			is_in_faction = no
			has_war = no
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 95
				owns_state = 194
			}
		}
		WHR = {
			is_subject = no
			is_in_faction = no
			has_war = no
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 93
				owns_state = 997
				owns_state = 241
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_WHR_poster
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_WHR_treaty option = UKR_WHR_TREATY_FAIL }
				}
			}
		}		
		WHR = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = WHR_allies days = 30 value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.12
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_WHR_treaty option = UKR_WHR_TREATY_GUARANTEED }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_WHR_treaty option = UKR_WHR_TREATY_GUARANTEES }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_WHR_treaty option = UKR_WHR_TREATY_HOMEL }
				}
			}
		}					
		add_political_power = -25
	}	
}

country_event = { # West Ukraine
	id = ukrfor.34
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.34" }
	title = ukrfor.34.t
	desc = ukrfor.34.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.34.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_How_much_land_var = 3 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						state = 80
						state = 89
						state = 1140
						state = 91
					}
					is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_What_austria_terms_var = 1 } }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_polish_autonomy }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_How_much_land_var = 2 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						state = 80
						state = 89
						state = 1140
					}
					is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_What_austria_terms_var = 1 } }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_polish_autonomy }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					is_east_galicia = yes
					is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_What_austria_terms_var = 1 } }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_polish_autonomy }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.UKR_AUS_What_austria_terms_var = 3 }
			}
			UKR = { 
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { has_guaranteed = ROOT }
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
				GER_remove_from_mitteleuropa = yes
				MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
				remove_from_all_tech_sharing_groups = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = URK
		}
		else = {
			UKR = { add_ideas = UKR_excessive_trade_with_austria }
			add_ideas = AUS_UKR_excessive_trade_with_austria
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = UKR
				modifier = KR_trade_agreement
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = UKR
				modifier = KR_trade_agreement
			}
		}
	}	
}

			}
		}

				FROM = { ROOT_is_threatened = yes }

country_event = { #Ultimatum for Cholm
	id = ukrfor.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.200" }
	title = ukrfor.200.t
	desc = ukrfor.200.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.200.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				1088 = {
					owner = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			1088 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = {
						id = ukrfor.203
						days = 1
						random = 24
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.201
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.200.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.202
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

}

	title = ukrfor.201.t
	desc = ukrfor.201.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ukrfor.201.a #great

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {

						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						AND = {
							is_claimed_by = ROM
							ROOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROM }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ukrfor.210.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ukrfor.210.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				WHR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			WHR = {
				country_event = {
					id = ukrfor.213
					days = 1
					random = 24
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.211
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

			factor = 75
		}
		FROM = {

			}
		}

country_event = { #
	id = ukrfor.230
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.230" }
	title = ukrfor.230.t
	desc = ukrfor.230.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_zluka

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.230.a #we will show them!
		FROM = {
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = PREV }
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = PREV }
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}				
			}
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_political_power = 200
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.15
		annex_country = {
			target = FROM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrmisc.62
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}	
}


country_event = { #ROM-UKR peace deal
	id = ukrfor.231
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.231" }
	title = ukrfor.231.t
	
	title = {
		text = ukrfor.231.t.victory
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.231.d.victory
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM }
	}
	
	title = {
		text = ukrfor.231.t.defeat
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.231.d.defeat
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_war_with = 202.owner
		owns_state = 78
		owns_state = 1222
		owns_state = 1320
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_enemy_tag = 202.owner }
		var:UKR_enemy_tag = {
			is_ukrainian_tag = yes
			is_valid_peace_target = yes
		}
		OR = {
			#Romania loses
			var:UKR_enemy_tag = {
				controls_state = 78 #Bessarabia
				controls_state = 1222 # Bujak
				controls_state = 1320 # 
				controls_state = 79 #Moldavia
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.15
			#Romania wins
			var:UKR_enemy_tag = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
			controls_state = 202 #Kyiv
			controls_state = 226 #Ekaterinoslav
			AND = {
				controls_state = 192 #Odessa
				controls_state = 791 #Podolia
				OR = {
					controls_state = 197 #Kherson
					controls_state = 198 #Vinnitsa
					controls_state = 1245 #Bratslav
					controls_state = 199 #Proskurov
					controls_state = 1241 #Pobuzhie
					controls_state = 1233 #Elisavetgrad
					controls_state = 1232 #Nikolayev
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_ROM_offered_peace }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = { flag = UKR_ROM_offered_peace days = 90 value = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					surrender_progress > 0.15
					NOT = { controls_state = 78 }
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = { flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM days = 60 value = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.231.a #We have no choice; send word to Moscow.
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
		var:219.owner = {

						limit = {

						}
						state = 80 #Cernauti
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			FROM = { add_to_array = { global.UKR_integration_state_array = PREV } }

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Elections
	id = ukrel.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrel.10" }

	desc = ukrel.10.d

		tag = UKR
		has_country_flag = UKR_presidential_elections
		UKR_vasyl_in_power = no
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_mapa
	
	option = {
		name = ukrel.10.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_oppositional_dyrektoria }

		}
		if = {

			}

	}

		trigger = { KR_mizhmoria_vote_passes = no }
	}
	desc = {
		text = mizhmoria.4.d.yes
		trigger = { KR_mizhmoria_vote_passes = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = mizhmoria.4.d.no
		trigger = { KR_mizhmoria_vote_passes = no }
	}

		name = mizhmoria.4.a
		trigger = { KR_mizhmoria_vote_passes = yes }

		set_country_flag = KR_joined_iea
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
			}
			country_event = mizhmoria.47
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
				set_country_flag = { flag = disable_ai_joining days = 1 value = 35 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.mizhmoria_tags_array
				country_event = { id = mizhmoria.47 days = KR_vote_delay }
				add_to_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }
			}
			set_variable = { ROOT.mizhmoria_pp_pool = 200 }
			add_to_variable = { global.mizhmoria_pp_pool = 200 }
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = mizhmoria.4.b
		trigger = { KR_mizhmoria_vote_passes = no }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.1
	}

			add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iece_education
		}

			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
			}
			country_event = mizhmoria.45
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
				set_country_flag = { flag = disable_ai_joining days = 1 value = 35 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.mizhmoria_tags_array
				country_event = { id = mizhmoria.45 days = KR_vote_delay }
				add_to_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }
			}
		}			
	}

		add_stability = -0.1

			}

			}

				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_trade_opinion = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_socialist_agriculture
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = UKR }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_add_trade_opinion = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_agriculture
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
			}
			country_event = mizhmoria.40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }

				country_event = { id = mizhmoria.40 days = KR_vote_delay }
				add_to_temp_variable = { KR_vote_delay = 1 }

country_event = { # 
	id = mizhmoria.40
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mizhmoria.40" }
	title = mizhmoria.40.t
	desc = mizhmoria.40.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3
	trigger = { has_country_flag = mizhmoria_member }
	
	option = {
		name = mizhmoria.40.a		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_conservative_agriculture
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_socialist_agriculture
						OR = {
							has_government = social_conservative
							has_authoritarian_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_conservative_agriculture
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_socialist_agriculture
						has_government = market_liberal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_conservative_agriculture }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = UKR }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_add_consumer_goods = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_trade_opinion = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_resource_penalty = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_conservative_agriculture
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_socialist_agriculture }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = UKR }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_pp = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_add_trade_opinion = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_out_of_supply = yes
				UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_socialist_agriculture
			}
		}

				check_variable = {
					var = ROOT.num_of_factories
					value = MIZ.num_of_factories
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_economy_transitional_period_amendment }
			hidden_effect = { add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1 }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_transitional
				days = 365
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = after_idea_expires
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = KR_mizhmoria_central_bank }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1
						add_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_3
					}
				}
				else = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1
						add_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KR_mizhmoria_central_bank }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1
					add_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_3
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1
					add_idea = KR_mizhmoria_iea_2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { 
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = KR_mizhmoria_central_bank }
					add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iea_3 
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iea_2
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MIZ_currency_zone
		MIZ = { country_event = mizhmoria.56 }
	}
	option = {
		name = mizhmoria.55.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KR_mizhmoria_central_bank }
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1a 
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KR_mizhmoria_iea_1
			}
		}
		MIZ = { country_event = mizhmoria.57 }
	}

		}

					array = global.mizhmoria_tags_array
					country_event = { id = mizhmoria.88 days = KR_vote_delay }

				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = mizhmoria.88
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { KR_is_mizhmoria_member = yes }
					country_event = mizhmoria.88
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_parties_formed }
					KR_mizhmoria_calculate_parties_support = yes
					country_event = {
						id = mizhmoria.89

				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_member_delegations_formed }

				}

		}

				for_each_scope_loop = {

country_event = { #Health cooperation - voting
	id = mizhmoria.88
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mizhmoria.88 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = mizhmoria.88.t
	desc = mizhmoria.88.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Not voting
		name = mizhmoria.88.a
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		}		
	}
	option = { #Yes
		name = mizhmoria.88.b
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.mizhmoria_yes_votes = ROOT.member_seats }
		KR_mizhmoria_dirty = yes
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = mizhmoria.88.c
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.mizhmoria_no_votes = ROOT.member_seats }
		KR_mizhmoria_dirty = yes
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = mizhmoria.88.e
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.mizhmoria_abstain_votes = ROOT.member_seats }
		KR_mizhmoria_dirty = yes
	}
}

	desc = mizhmoria.90.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	option = { #Not voting
		name = mizhmoria.90.a
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		}		
	}
	option = { #Yes
		name = mizhmoria.90.b
		trigger = { has_global_flag = UKR_mizhmoria_federal_national_curias_formed }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}

	}

			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				OR = {
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.mizhmoria_no_votes = ROOT.member_seats }
		KR_mizhmoria_dirty = yes
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = mizhmoria.90.e

			}
		}

		KR_mizhmoria_dirty = yes
